<td>3 acts

<td>1876
</td></tr>

</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Ballets&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Ballets</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For orchestra</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="18 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the orchestra</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_piano&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the piano</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_piano_4_hands&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the piano 4 hands</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Sylvia
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td class="wi_head">The Nymph of Diana

<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>

</td></tr>

</li></ul>

</dd><dd>2. Les faunes et dryades
</dd><dd>3. Le berger
</dd><dd>4. Grand pas des chasseresses
</dd><dd>5. Intermezzo
</dd><dd>6. Valse lente
</dd><dd>7. Scène
</dd><dd>8. Cortège rustique
</dd><dd>9. Scène
</dd><dd>10. Finale—Entrée du sorcier
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act II
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>11. Entr’acte
</dd><dd>12. La grotte d’Orion
</dd><dd>13. Pas des Éthiopiens
</dd><dd>14. Chant bacchique
</dd><dd>15. Scène et danse de la Bacchante
</dd><dd>16. Scène finale
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act III
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>17. Grand cortège de Bacchus
</dd><dd>18. Scène
</dd><dd>19. Danse barcarolle
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Divertissement</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>20. Variation dansée (Pizzicati)
</dd><dd>21. Pas d’andante
</dd><dd>22. Pas des esclaves
</dd><dd>23. Variation dansée (valse)
</dd><dd>24. Galop générale
</dd><dd>25. Finale—Le temple De Diane
</dd><dd>26. Apothéose—L’apparition d’Endymion
</dd></dl>
